Update your local business listing once, and the changes appear across all the sites.\n           </div>\n\n         </div>\n      </div>\n\n</div>\n      </div>\n\n</div>\n<div data-id=\"scanner\" data-lazy-image=\"{&quot;src&quot;:&quot;https://img1.wsimg.com/Sitecore/C/7/photo-get-found-scan-web-stnd.jpg&quot;,&quot;type&quot;:&quot;background&quot;,&quot;hideAtWidthBelow&quot;:&quot;0&quot;,&quot;hideAtWidthAbove&quot;:&quot;0&quot;}\" class=\"vsc-get-found-scanner-module background-container \">\n    <div class=\"l-main-container title-center\">\n        <iframe class=\"locu-iframe\" src=\"https://locu.godaddy.com/scanner/autocomplete_iframe?regionsite=www&amp;marketid=en-US\" allowtransparency=\"true\"></iframe>\n    </div>\n</div>\n<div data-id=\"faq\" class=\"vsc-accordion-module faq-accordion-wrap tile-section bg-faint \">\n  <div class=\"container\">\n    <div class=\"row\">\n      <div class=\"col-sm-12\">\n        <h2 class=\"text-center h1\">\nYour questions, our answers.        </h2>\n        <ul class=\"faq-group list-unstyled\">\n                  <li class=\"faq-item\">\n                    <h3 class=\"faq-content-title headline-primary\">\nWhat does it matter if my business information is listed incorrectly online?                    </h3>\n                    <div style=\"overflow: hidden;\" class=\"faq-content\">\nThe cost of inaccurate information online is actually quite high. In fact, you could lose out on potential sales. We've found that 68% of people will take their business elsewhere if they see missing or inaccurate internet advertising — open hours, phone number, address, prices — online.                    </div>\n                  </li>\n                  <li class=\"faq-item\">\n                    <h3 class=\"faq-content-title headline-primary\">\nHow much time will I need to spend creating local business listings using Get Found?                    </h3>\n                    <div style=\"overflow: hidden;\" class=\"faq-content\">\nGetting started is easy and usually takes less than 5 minutes – just complete two simple steps to get your basic business listing published across the web. If you choose to provide details such as menus, price lists, or item photos, you may need to spend anywhere from 10 minutes to an hour. The good news is that you only need to do this in one place to get it published on many sites. And the results are potentially huge.                    </div>\n                  </li>\n                  <li class=\"faq-item\">\n                    <h3 class=\"faq-content-title headline-primary\">\nWhat kind of information can Get Found publish about my business?                    </h3>\n                    <div style=\"overflow: hidden;\" class=\"faq-content\">\nGet Found can publish your business description, contact information (phone number, website address), hours of operation, menus and price lists, item photos and descriptions, payment and delivery options, amenities and more. This is exactly the type of internet advertising that customers want when looking for new local businesses. A detailed and consistent business listing online will help you stand out from the pack and attract customers to your business.                    </div>\n                  </li>\n                  <li class=\"faq-item\">\n                    <h3 class=\"faq-content-title headline-primary\">\nWhere will Get Found publish my local business listing?                    </h3>\n                    <div style=\"overflow: hidden;\" class=\"faq-content\">\nWe've established partnerships with some of the top consumer destination sites online. Currently, we publish to Google, Bing, Yelp, TripAdvisor, YP, Foursquare, Citysearch, and many other smaller sites. We're continually expanding our list of business listing partners — you'll be the first to know once we find more places to publish your business information.                    </div>\n                  </li>\n                  <li class=\"faq-item\">\n                    <h3 class=\"faq-content-title headline-primary\">\nWhat do you mean by \"publish\"?                    </h3>\n                    <div style=\"overflow: hidden;\" class=\"faq-content\">\nBy \"publish\" your business information, we mean displaying it on all of our partner sites for you (and on your own website if you choose to use our widget to display your content there). To share or update your business listing with GoDaddy Get Found, all you do is click a single <strong>Publish</strong> button and your information appears on all our partner sites.                    </div>\n                  </li>\n                  <li class=\"faq-item\">\n                    <h3 class=\"faq-content-title headline-primary\">\nWhat kind of business is this for?                    </h3>\n                    <div style=\"overflow: hidden;\" class=\"faq-content\">\nDo you have a physical location that customers visit (ex. restaurant, spa, salon)? Or, do you serve a local area without a physical location that customers visit (ex. plumber, food struck, boat charter)? If so, Get Found is for you. We are not yet able to serve businesses who operate online and do not have a physical address to share (ex. web designer, ecommerce store, consultant), but that is coming in the future.                    </div>\n                  </li>\n                  <li class=\"faq-item\">\n                    <h3 class=\"faq-content-title headline-primary\">\nHow long will it take for my business listing to get published?                    </h3>\n                    <div style=\"overflow: hidden;\" class=\"faq-content\">\nWhen you submit your business listing to Get Found, one of our dedicated data specialists reviews your data and makes sure everything is ready to go to our partner sites. Your data is then shared with our partners. Some of our partner sites will publish your local listing in as little as a few days; others will take up to eight weeks.                    </div>\n                  </li>\n                  <li class=\"faq-item\">\n                    <h3 class=\"faq-content-title headline-primary\">\nTell me more about how I can use your widget to display my menus or price lists on my own site.                    </h3>\n                    <div style=\"overflow: hidden;\" class=\"faq-content\">\nTo share your menus or price lists on your own website, you need to install a short snippet of HTML to the webpage where you want your menus or lists to appear. We even provide you with several designer templates to choose from. If you want, you can edit the look and feel of the templates to match the existing style of your website. Oh, and they're mobile-compatible too, so you can be sure that your menus or price lists will look great on all devices.                    </div>\n                  </li>\n                  <li class=\"faq-item\">\n                    <h3 class=\"faq-content-title headline-primary\">\nWhat if I don't have a website?                    </h3>\n                    <div style=\"overflow: hidden;\" class=\"faq-content\">\nThat's totally fine. We'll still publish your information on all of our partner sites — it's actually the best way to get your business discovered online when you don't have a website. Want a great-looking website you build yourself? Check out <a href=\"https://www.godaddy.com/websites/website-builder?ci=92937\">GoDaddy Website Builder.</a>                    </div>\n                  </li>\n                  <li class=\"faq-item\">\n                    <h3 class=\"faq-content-title headline-primary\">\nAre there any system requirements for using GoDaddy Get Found?                    </h3>\n                    <div style=\"overflow: hidden;\" class=\"faq-content\">\nGoDaddy Get Found works best in Google Chrome, but is also supported on Firefox, Safari, and Internet Explorer.                    </div>\n                  </li>\n        </ul>\n\n          <div class=\"faq-btn-wrap text-center hidden-xs\">\n              \n  <a href=\"#\" class=\"btn btn-default faq-modal-btn \" data-eid=\"gce.sales.online-marketing/local-business-listings.accordion.faq_accordion_module.link.10933a1c-3880-455d-a2d7-6861a21133e6\" data-tdata=\"module_location,4^block_path,/ComponentSettings/GoDaddy/Sales/online-marketing/local-business-listings/FAQ Accordion Module/Primary CTA^block_version,1^block_sequence,1^campaign_name,^split_id,^split_side,\">\n    <div class=\" \"></div>\n    <div class=\"\">See all</div>\n  </a>\n\n          </div>\n      </div>\n\n        <div class=\"accordion-modal\" style=\"display:none\" data-modal-title=\"\">\n            <h4>\nWhat does it matter if my business information is listed incorrectly online?            </h4>\n            <div class=\"accordion-modal-text\">\nThe cost of inaccurate information online is actually quite high. In fact, you could lose out on potential sales. We've found that 68% of people will take their business elsewhere if they see missing or inaccurate internet advertising — open hours, phone number, address, prices — online.            </div>\n            <h4>\nHow much time will I need to spend creating local business listings using Get Found?            </h4>\n            <div class=\"accordion-modal-text\">\nGetting started is easy and usually takes less than 5 minutes – just complete two simple steps to get your basic business listing published across the web. If you choose to provide details such as menus, price lists, or item photos, you may need to spend anywhere from 10 minutes to an hour. The good news is that you only need to do this in one place to get it published on many sites. And the results are potentially huge.            </div>\n            <h4>\nWhat kind of information can Get Found publish about my business?            </h4>\n            <div class=\"accordion-modal-text\">\nGet Found can publish your business description, contact information (phone number, website address), hours of operation, menus and price lists, item photos and descriptions, payment and delivery options, amenities and more. This is exactly the type of internet advertising that customers want when looking for new local businesses. A detailed and consistent business listing online will help you stand out from the pack and attract customers to your business.            </div>\n            <h4>\nWhere will Get Found publish my local business listing?            </h4>\n            <div class=\"accordion-modal-text\">\nWe've established partnerships with some of the top consumer destination sites online. Currently, we publish to Google, Bing, Yelp, TripAdvisor, YP, Foursquare, Citysearch, and many other smaller sites. We're continually expanding our list of business listing partners — you'll be the first to know once we find more places to publish your business information.            </div>\n            <h4>\nWhat do you mean by \"publish\"?            </h4>\n            <div class=\"accordion-modal-text\">\nBy \"publish\" your business information, we mean displaying it on all of our partner sites for you (and on your own website if you choose to use our widget to display your content there). To share or update your business listing with GoDaddy Get Found, all you do is click a single <strong>Publish</strong> button and your information appears on all our partner sites.            </div>\n            <h4>\nWhat kind of business is this for?            </h4>\n            <div class=\"accordion-modal-text\">\nDo you have a physical location that customers visit (ex. restaurant, spa, salon)? Or, do you serve a local area without a physical location that customers visit (ex. plumber, food struck, boat charter)? If so, Get Found is for you. We are not yet able to serve businesses who operate online and do not have a physical address to share (ex. web designer, ecommerce store, consultant), but that is coming in the future.            </div>\n            <h4>\nHow long will it take for my business listing to get published?            </h4>\n            <div class=\"accordion-modal-text\">\nWhen you submit your business listing to Get Found, one of our dedicated data specialists reviews your data and makes sure everything is ready to go to our partner sites. Your data is then shared with our partners. Some of our partner sites will publish your local listing in as little as a few days; others will take up to eight weeks.            </div>\n            <h4>\nTell me more about how I can use your widget to display my menus or price lists on my own site.            </h4>\n            <div class=\"accordion-modal-text\">\nTo share your menus or price lists on your own website, you need to install a short snippet of HTML to the webpage where you want your menus or lists to appear. We even provide you with several designer templates to choose from. If you want, you can edit the look and feel of the templates to match the existing style of your website. Oh, and they're mobile-compatible too, so you can be sure that your menus or price lists will look great on all devices.            </div>\n            <h4>\nWhat if I don't have a website?            </h4>\n            <div class=\"accordion-modal-text\">\nThat's totally fine. We'll still publish your information on all of our partner sites — it's actually the best way to get your business discovered online when you don't have a website. Want a great-looking website you build yourself? Check out <a href=\"https://www.godaddy.com/websites/website-builder?ci=92937\">GoDaddy Website Builder.</a>            </div>\n            <h4>\nAre there any system requirements for using GoDaddy Get Found?            </h4>\n            <div class=\"accordion-modal-text\">\nGoDaddy Get Found works best in Google Chrome, but is also supported on Firefox, Safari, and Internet Explorer.            </div>\n        </div>\n    </div>\n  </div>\n</div><div data-id=\"\" class=\"vsc-disclaimer-module disclaimers-row bg-faint \">\n  <div class=\"container\">\n    <div class=\"row\">\n      <div class=\"col-sm-12\">\n        <span>4</span>\n        <a href=\"#\" class=\"simple-link disclaimers-modal-link\">Disclaimers</a>\n        <div class=\"disclaimers-text\"></div>\n      </div>\n    </div>\n  </div>\n  <div class=\"disclaimers-modal\" style=\"display: none;\" data-modal-title=\"Disclaimers\">\n      <p>4 Product renewal pricing subject to change.</p>\n    <p></p>\n  </div>\n</div>\n</div>\n<div id=\"footer\"><div id=\"gtm_privacy\"></div><div id=\"footer-support\"><div class=\"container\"><h4 class=\"font-primary-bold\"><div class=\"support-full\">Need help?&nbsp;\nCall our award-winning support team 24/7 at&nbsp;<span id=\"footer-support-phone\">(480) 505-8877</span></div><span class=\"support-short\">Need help?
